@pytest.mark.test_p0
def test_I2_20_3(indigo2_obj, request, init_ota_tests):
"""Test HMI OTA update.

This test should be provided with UBD for HMI OTA package with
signature different than the currently installed build.

Expected:
The OTA update from this url should fail because of signature
mismatch.
"""
test_case_no = get_test_case_no_for_report(request)
logging.info("Test case: I2.20.3 - OTA update HMI: Inside function")
test_result = -1
buildtype = indigo2_obj.get_build_type()

# Use user build UBD for userdebug and vice-versa. This should create
# signature mismatch scenario.
if buildtype == "userdebug":
ubdpath = "http://fw.whrcloud.com/test/test/ees/CrossCategory/Indigo2/W00101103/1113/W00101103.json.signed.enc"
else:
